fib_slice_bicat C₂ → fib_slice_bicat C₁

∏ a b : fib_slice_bicat C₂,
fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ a, b ⟧
→ fib_slice_bicat C₁ ⟦ ?F₀ a, ?F₀ b ⟧
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
∏ (a b : fib_slice_bicat C₂)
(f g : fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ a, b ⟧),
f ==> g → ?F₁ a b f ==> ?F₁ a b g
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
∏ a : fib_slice_bicat C₂,
id₁ (?F₀ a) ==> ?F₁ a a (id₁ a)
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
∏ (a b c : fib_slice_bicat C₂)
(f : fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ a, b ⟧)
(g : fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ b, c ⟧),
?F₁ a b f · ?F₁ b c g ==> ?F₁ a c (f · g)

F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
fib_slice_bicat C₂ → fib_slice_bicat C₁
 exact (λ D, cleaving_of_cleaving_lift_obj D F).

id₁
  ((λ D : fib_slice_bicat C₂,

C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
∏ (a b c : fib_slice_bicat C₂)
(f : fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ a, b ⟧)
(g : fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ b, c ⟧),
(λ (D₁ D₂ : fib_slice_bicat C₂)
 (G : fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧),
 reindex_of_cartesian_disp_functor F G (pr2 D₁)) a b f
· (λ (D₁ D₂ : fib_slice_bicat C₂)
   (G : fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧),
   reindex_of_cartesian_disp_functor F G (pr2 D₁)) b c
    g ==>
(λ (D₁ D₂ : fib_slice_bicat C₂)
 (G : fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧),
 reindex_of_cartesian_disp_functor F G (pr2 D₁)) a c
  (f · g)
 exact (λ D₁ D₂ D₃ G₁ G₂, reindex_of_disp_functor_composite F (pr1 G₁) (pr1 G₂)).
  Defined.

  reindex_fib_psfunctor_data (id₂ G) =

C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
∏ (x : C₁)

PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
  reindex_fib_psfunctor_data (id₂ G) x xx =

C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportb
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
   pr1 G (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G (F x) xx)
  (functor_id F x) (id_disp (pr1 G (F x) xx)) =
transportb (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (G (F x) xx))
  (functor_id F x) (id_disp (G (F x) xx))

      apply idpath.
    
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
psfunctor_vcomp2_law reindex_fib_psfunctor_data
 
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁, G₂, G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
α: G₁ ==> G₂
β: G₂ ==> G₃
PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
  reindex_fib_psfunctor_data (α • β) =
PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
  reindex_fib_psfunctor_data α
• PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
    reindex_fib_psfunctor_data β

D₁, D₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁, G₂, G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
α: G₁ ==> G₂
β: G₂ ==> G₃
∏ (x : C₁)
(xx : pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x),
PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
  reindex_fib_psfunctor_data (α • β) x xx =
(PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
   reindex_fib_psfunctor_data α
 • PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
     reindex_fib_psfunctor_data β) x xx

      
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁, G₂, G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
α: G₁ ==> G₂
β: G₂ ==> G₃
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportb
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
   pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
  (functor_id F x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
      pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof (F x))
     (α (F x) xx ;; β (F x) xx)%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₁ (F x) xx -->[ # F z] G₃ (F x) xx)
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportb (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (G₃ (F x) xx))
     (functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportb
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
         pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)
        (functor_id F x) (α (F x) xx) ;; transportb
                                           (λ z : 
                                               C₂
                                               ⟦ F x,
                                               F x ⟧,
                                            pr1 G₂
                                              (F x) xx -->[
                                            z] pr1 G₃
                                                 (F x)
                                                 xx)
                                           (functor_id
                                              F x)
                                           (β (F x) xx))%mor_disp)

      
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁, G₂, G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
α: G₁ ==> G₂
β: G₂ ==> G₃
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
   pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
  (! functor_id F x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
      pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof (F x))
     (α (F x) xx ;; β (F x) xx)%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₁ (F x) xx -->[ # F z] G₃ (F x) xx)
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportf (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (G₃ (F x) xx))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
         pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)
        (! functor_id F x) (α (F x) xx) ;; transportf
                                             (λ z : 
                                                 C₂
                                                 ⟦ 
                                                 F x,
                                                 F x ⟧,
                                              pr1 G₂
                                                (F x)
                                                xx -->[
                                              z] pr1
                                                 G₃
                                                 (F x)
                                                 xx)
                                             (! functor_id
                                                 F x)
                                             (β (F x)
                                                xx))%mor_disp)

      
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁, G₂, G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
α: G₁ ==> G₂
β: G₂ ==> G₃
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
   pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
  (! functor_id F x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
      pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof (F x))
     (α (F x) xx ;; β (F x) xx)%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₁ (F x) xx -->[ # F z] G₃ (F x) xx)
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportf (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (G₃ (F x) xx))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (pr1 G₃ (F x) xx))
        (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x))
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
            pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)
           (! functor_id F x) (α (F x) xx) ;; β (F x)
                                                xx)%mor_disp))

      
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁, G₂, G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
α: G₁ ==> G₂
β: G₂ ==> G₃
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
   pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
  (! functor_id F x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
      pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof (F x))
     (α (F x) xx ;; β (F x) xx)%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₁ (F x) xx -->[ # F z] G₃ (F x) xx)
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportf (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (G₃ (F x) xx))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (pr1 G₃ (F x) xx))
        (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x))
        (transportf
           (mor_disp (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)
              (pr1 G₃ (F x) xx))
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x))
              (# F (id₁ x)) (id₁ (F x))
              (! functor_id F x))
           (α (F x) xx ;; β (F x) xx)%mor_disp)))

D₁, D₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁, G₂, G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
α: G₁ ==> G₂
β: G₂ ==> G₃
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (G₃ (F x) xx))
  (maponpaths # F
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x))
  (transportf (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (G₃ (F x) xx))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (pr1 G₃ (F x) xx))
        (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x))
        (transportf
           (mor_disp (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)
              (pr1 G₃ (F x) xx))
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x))
              (# F (id₁ x)) (id₁ (F x))
              (! functor_id F x))
           (α (F x) xx ;; β (F x) xx)%mor_disp))) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
   pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
  (! functor_id F x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
      pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof (F x))
     (α (F x) xx ;; β (F x) xx)%mor_disp)

cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x)) (# F (id₁ x))
  (id₁ (F x)) (! functor_id F x) @
maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x))) (! functor_id F x) @
! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x) @
maponpaths # F
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x) =

! functor_id F x

  ▹ # reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G)

transportb (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (G (F x) xx))
  (functor_id F x) (id_disp (G (F x) xx)) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G (F x) xx -->[ # F z] G (F x) xx)
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportb (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (G (F x) xx))
     (functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
         G (F x) xx -->[ (# F)%cat z] pr1 G (F x) xx)
        (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
        (transportb
           (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (pr1 G (F x) xx))
           (functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
           (♯ G
              (transportb
                 (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧, xx -->[ z] xx)
                 (functor_id F x) (id_disp xx)) ;; 
            transportb
              (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
               pr1 G (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G (F x) xx)
              (functor_id F x)
              (id_disp (pr1 G (F x) xx)))) ;; transportb
                                                (λ 
                                                 z : 
                                                 C₂
                                                 ⟦ 
                                                 F x,
                                                 F x ⟧,
                                                 pr1 G
                                                 (F x)
                                                 xx -->[
                                                 z] 
                                                 pr1 G
                                                 (F x)
                                                 xx)
                                                (functor_id
                                                 F x)
                                                (id_disp
                                                 (pr1
                                                 G
                                                 (F x)
                                                 xx)))%mor_disp)

runitor (# reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G) =
((# reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G
  ◃ PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_id
      reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₂)
 • PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
     reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G (id₁ D₂))
• PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
    reindex_fib_psfunctor_data (runitor G)

                                                (F x)
                                                xx)
                                          (! functor_id
                                               F x)
                                          (id_disp
                                             (pr1 G
                                                (F x)
                                                xx)))) ;; 
      transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
         pr1 G (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G (F x) xx)
        (! functor_id F x) (id_disp (pr1 G (F x) xx)))%mor_disp)

      
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (G (F x) xx))
  (! functor_id F x) (id_disp (G (F x) xx)) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G (F x) xx -->[ # F z] G (F x) xx)
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportf (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (G (F x) xx))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (pr1 G (F x) xx))
        (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x))
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
            G (F x) xx -->[
            (# F)%cat z] pr1 G (F x) xx)
           (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof
              x)
           (transportf
              (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (pr1 G (F x) xx))
              (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
              (transportf
                 (mor_disp (G (F x) xx)
                    (pr1 G (F x) xx))
                 (maponpaths
                    (compose ((# F)%cat (id₁ x)))
                    (! functor_id F x))
                 (transportf
                    (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
                     G (F x) xx -->[ z] G (F x) xx)
                    (! functor_id F x)
                    (id_disp (G (F x) xx)) ;; id_disp
                                                (pr1 G
                                                 (F x)
                                                 xx)))) ;; 
         id_disp (pr1 G (F x) xx))%mor_disp))

  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x) =

      apply homset_property.

G₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₃, D₄ ⟧
((# reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₁
  ◃ PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
      reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₂ G₃)
 • PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
     reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₁ (G₂ · G₃))
• PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells
    reindex_fib_psfunctor_data (lassociator G₁ G₂ G₃) =
(lassociator (# reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₁)
   (# reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₂)
   (# reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₃)
 • (PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
      reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₁ G₂
    ▹ # reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₃))
• PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
    reindex_fib_psfunctor_data (G₁ · G₂) G₃

F: C₁ ⟶ C₂

G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₃, D₄ ⟧
∏ (x : C₁)
(xx : pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x),
(((# reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₁
   ◃ PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
       reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₂ G₃)

 • PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_on_cells

  x xx =
((lassociator (# reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₁)
    (# reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₂)

     ▹ # reindex_fib_psfunctor_data G₃))

     reindex_fib_psfunctor_data (G₁ · G₂) G₃) x xx

      
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂, D₃, D₄: fib_slice_bicat C₂

G₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₃, D₄ ⟧
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
   # F z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
            (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportb
     (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
     (functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
         G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
         (# F)%cat z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
                        (pr1 G₂ (F x)
                           (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
        (transportb
           (mor_disp
              (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
              (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                 (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
           (functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
           (transportb
              (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
               pr1 G₃ (F x)
                 (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
               z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
              (functor_id F x)
              (id_disp
                 (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))) ;; 
            transportb
              (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
               pr1 G₃ (F x)
                 (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
               z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
              (functor_id F x)
              (id_disp
                 (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))))) ;;

  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[

     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
         G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
         (# F)%cat z] G₃ (F x)
                        (pr1 G₂ (F x)
                           (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
        (transportf
           (mor_disp
              (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
              (G₃ (F x)
                 (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
           (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
           (transportf
              (mor_disp
                 (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))

                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))))) ;;

C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂, D₃, D₄: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧

G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₃, D₄ ⟧
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf
  (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
     (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
  (maponpaths # F
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
         G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
         (# F)%cat z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
                        (pr1 G₂ (F x)
                           (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
        (transportf
           (mor_disp
              (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
              (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                 (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
           (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
           (transportf
              (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
               pr1 G₃ (F x)
                 (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
               z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
              (! functor_id F x)
              (id_disp
                 (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))) ;; 
            transportf
              (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
               pr1 G₃ (F x)
                 (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
               z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
              (! functor_id F x)
              (id_disp
                 (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))))) ;;

        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,

        (! functor_id F x)

      ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))

                 (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))))))) =

  (transportf
     (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
     (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
        (! functor_id F x) @
      ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportb
        (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
           (pr1 G₃ (F x)
              (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
        (id_right (# F (id₁ x)))
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
            G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
            # F z] G₃ (F x)
                     (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
           (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof
              x)
           (transportf
              (mor_disp
                 (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
                 (G₃ (F x)
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
              (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x))
                 (# F (id₁ x)) (# F (id₁ x))
                 (! functor_id F x) @
               ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
              (id_disp
                 (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))) ;; 
               ♯ G₃
                 (transportf
                    (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
                     pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx) -->[
                     z] pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))
                    (! functor_id F x)
                    (id_disp
                       (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))))%mor_disp))))

        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))))
     (! id_right (id₁ (F x)) @
      cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x)) (# F (id₁ x))
        (id₁ (F x)) (! functor_id F x) @
      maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
        (! functor_id F x) @
      ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (id_disp
        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))))) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
   # F z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
            (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
     (! id_right (# F (id₁ x)) @
      maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
        (! functor_id F x) @
      ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
         G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
         # F z] G₃ (F x)
                  (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
        (transportf
           (mor_disp
              (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))

                 (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))

D₁, D₂, D₃, D₄: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
G₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₃, D₄ ⟧
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf
  (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
     (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
  ((! id_right (# F (id₁ x)) @
    maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
      (! functor_id F x) @
    ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x)) @
   maponpaths # F
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x))
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
      G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
      # F z] G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
           (G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
        (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x))
           (# F (id₁ x)) (# F (id₁ x))
           (! functor_id F x) @
         ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
        (transportb
           (mor_disp
              (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
              (G₃ (F x)
                 (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
           (id_left (# F (id₁ x)))
           ((♯ G₃)%mor_disp
              (transportf
                 (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
                  pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx) -->[
                  z] pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))
                 (! functor_id F x)
                 (id_disp
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))))))) =
?b
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂, D₃, D₄: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
G₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
G₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₃, D₄ ⟧
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
?b =
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
     (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))))
  ((! id_right (id₁ (F x)) @
    cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x)) (# F (id₁ x))
      (id₁ (F x)) (! functor_id F x) @
    maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
      (! functor_id F x) @
    ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x)) @
   maponpaths # F
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x) @
   ! id_right (# F (id₁ x)) @
   maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
     (! functor_id F x) @
   ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x) @
   maponpaths # F
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x))
  (id_disp (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))))

   H₁ (F x) (G (F x) xx) -->[
   # F z] pr1 H₂ (F x) (pr1 G (F x) xx))
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (H₁ (F x) (G (F x) xx))
        (pr1 H₂ (F x) (pr1 G (F x) xx)))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (H₁ (F x) (G (F x) xx))
           (pr1 H₂ (F x) (pr1 G (F x) xx)))
        (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x))
        (transportf
           (mor_disp (pr1 H₁ (F x) (G (F x) xx))
              (pr1 H₂ (F x) (pr1 G (F x) xx)))
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x))
              (# F (id₁ x)) (id₁ (F x))
              (! functor_id F x))
           (α (F x) (G (F x) xx) ;; id_disp
                                      (pr1 H₂ (F x)
                                         (pr1 G (F x)
                                            xx)))%mor_disp)))

     (mor_disp (H₁ (F x) (G (F x) xx))
        (pr1 H₂ (F x) (pr1 G (F x) xx)))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (H₁ (F x) (G (F x) xx))
           (pr1 H₂ (F x) (pr1 G (F x) xx)))
        (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x))
        (transportf
           (mor_disp (pr1 H₁ (F x) (pr1 G (F x) xx))
              (pr1 H₂ (F x) (pr1 G (F x) xx)))
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x))
              (# F (id₁ x)) (id₁ (F x))
              (! functor_id F x))
           (transportf
              (mor_disp
                 (pr1 H₁ (F x) (pr1 G (F x) xx))
                 (pr1 H₂ (F x) (pr1 G (F x) xx)))
              (! id_left (id₁ (F x)))
              (α (F x) (pr1 G (F x) xx))))))

           (! functor_id F x))
        (♯ H
           (transportf
              (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
               pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)
              (! functor_id F x) (α (F x) xx)) ;; 
         id_disp (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))%mor_disp))

      
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂, D₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁, G₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
H: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
α: G₁ ==> G₂
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   H (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx) -->[
   # F z] pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx))
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (H (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))
        (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (H (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))
           (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))
        (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x))

           (transportf
              (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,

              (! functor_id F x) (α (F x) xx)) ;; 
         id_disp (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))%mor_disp)) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (H (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))
     (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))
  (maponpaths # F
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (H (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))
        (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf

           (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))

           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x))
              (# F (id₁ x)) (id₁ (F x))
              (! functor_id F x))
           (id_disp (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)) ;; 
            ♯ (pr1 H) (α (F x) xx))%mor_disp)))

G₁, G₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
H: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
α: G₁ ==> G₂
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf
  (mor_disp (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))
     (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))
  (maponpaths # (functor_identity C₂)
     (! functor_id F x) @
   ! id_right (# F (id₁ x)) @
   maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
     (! functor_id F x) @
   ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x) @
   maponpaths # F
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x))
  ((♯ (pr1 H))%mor_disp (α (F x) xx)) =
transportf
  (mor_disp (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))
     (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))
  (! id_left (id₁ (F x)) @
   cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x)) (# F (id₁ x))
     (id₁ (F x)) (! functor_id F x) @
   maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
     (! functor_id F x) @
   ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x) @
   maponpaths # F
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x))
  ((♯ (pr1 H))%mor_disp (α (F x) xx))

      
C₁, C₂: univalent_category
F: C₁ ⟶ C₂
D₁, D₂, D₃: fib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁, G₂: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
H: fib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
α: G₁ ==> G₂
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_fib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
maponpaths # (functor_identity C₂) (! functor_id F x) @
! id_right (# F (id₁ x)) @
maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x))) (! functor_id F x) @
! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x) @
maponpaths # F
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x) =
! id_left (id₁ (F x)) @
cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x)) (# F (id₁ x))
  (id₁ (F x)) (! functor_id F x) @
maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x))) (! functor_id F x) @
! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x) @
maponpaths # F
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)

      apply homset_property.
  Qed.

C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats

α: G₁ ==> G₂

x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportb
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
   pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
  (functor_id F x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
      pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof (F x))
     (α (F x) xx ;; β (F x) xx)%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₁ (F x) xx -->[ # F z] G₃ (F x) xx)
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportb (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (G₃ (F x) xx))
     (functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportb
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
         pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)
        (functor_id F x) (α (F x) xx) ;; transportb
                                           (λ z : 
                                               C₂
                                               ⟦ F x,
                                               F x ⟧,
                                            pr1 G₂
                                              (F x) xx -->[
                                            z] pr1 G₃
                                                 (F x)
                                                 xx)
                                           (functor_id
                                              F x)
                                           (β (F x) xx))%mor_disp)

F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧

  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,

  (! functor_id F x)

      pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)

  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportf (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (G₃ (F x) xx))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
         pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)
        (! functor_id F x) (α (F x) xx) ;; transportf
                                             (λ z : 
                                                 C₂
                                                 ⟦ 
                                                 F x,
                                                 F x ⟧,
                                              pr1 G₂
                                                (F x)
                                                xx -->[
                                              z] pr1
                                                 G₃
                                                 (F x)

                                             (! functor_id
                                                 F x)

                                                xx))%mor_disp)

      
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
D₁, D₂: opfib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁, G₂, G₃: opfib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
α: G₁ ==> G₂
β: G₂ ==> G₃
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf
  (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
   pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
  (! functor_id F x)
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
      pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₃ (F x) xx)
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof (F x))
     (α (F x) xx ;; β (F x) xx)%mor_disp) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₁ (F x) xx -->[ # F z] G₃ (F x) xx)
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportf (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (G₃ (F x) xx))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (G₁ (F x) xx) (pr1 G₃ (F x) xx))
        (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x))
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
            pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)
           (! functor_id F x) (α (F x) xx) ;; β (F x)
                                                xx)%mor_disp))

cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x)) (# F (id₁ x))
  (id₁ (F x)) (! functor_id F x) @
maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x))) (! functor_id F x) @
! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x) @
maponpaths # F
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x) =
disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof (F x) @
! functor_id F x

      apply homset_property.

  ▹ # reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data G)

transportb (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (G (F x) xx))
  (functor_id F x) (id_disp (G (F x) xx)) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G (F x) xx -->[ # F z] G (F x) xx)
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportb (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (G (F x) xx))
     (functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
         G (F x) xx -->[ (# F)%cat z] pr1 G (F x) xx)
        (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
        (transportb
           (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (pr1 G (F x) xx))
           (functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
           (♯ G
              (transportb
                 (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧, xx -->[ z] xx)
                 (functor_id F x) (id_disp xx)) ;; 
            transportb
              (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
               pr1 G (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G (F x) xx)
              (functor_id F x)
              (id_disp (pr1 G (F x) xx)))) ;; transportb
                                                (λ 
                                                 z :

                                                 z]

                                                 xx)
                                                (functor_id
                                                 F x)
                                                (id_disp
                                                 (pr1
                                                 G
                                                 (F x)
                                                 xx)))%mor_disp)

                 (transportf
                    (mor_disp (G (F x) xx)
                       (pr1 G (F x) xx))
                    (maponpaths
                       (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
                       (! functor_id F x))
                    (transportf
                       (mor_disp (G (F x) xx)
                          (pr1 G (F x) xx))
                       (! id_right (# F (id₁ x)))
                       ((♯ G)%mor_disp
                          (transportf
                             (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
                              xx -->[ z] xx)
                             (! functor_id F x)
                             (id_disp xx))))))))))

  ((♯ (pr1 G))%mor_disp (id_disp xx)) =
transportf (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (G (F x) xx))
  (! functor_id F x) (id_disp (G (F x) xx))

((# reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data G
  ◃ PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_id
      reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data D₂)
 • PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
     reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data G (id₁ D₂))

    reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data (runitor G)

     (functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,

           (mor_disp (G (F x) xx) (pr1 G (F x) xx))
           (functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))

            (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
         G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
         (# F)%cat z] G₃ (F x)
                        (pr1 G₂ (F x)
                           (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
        (transportf
           (mor_disp
              (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
              (G₃ (F x)
                 (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
           (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
           (transportf
              (mor_disp
                 (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
                 (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))))
              (! functor_id F x)
              (id_disp
                 (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))) ;; 
            ♯ G₃
              (transportf
                 (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
                  pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx) -->[
                  z] pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))
                 (! functor_id F x)
                 (id_disp
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))))) ;; 
      transportf
        (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
         pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
         z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
              (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (! functor_id F x)
        (id_disp
           (pr1 G₃ (F x)
              (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))))%mor_disp)

F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧

xx: pr1 (reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf
  (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))

     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x))

        (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
           (pr1 G₃ (F x)
              (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
        (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x))
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
            G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
            (# F)%cat z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
                           (pr1 G₂ (F x)
                              (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
           (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof
              x)
           (transportf
              (mor_disp
                 (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))

                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))

                    (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
                    (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                       (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
                 (maponpaths
                    (compose ((# F)%cat (id₁ x)))
                    (! functor_id F x))
                 (transportf
                    (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
                     pr1 G₃ (F x)
                       (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
                     z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
                          (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
                    (! functor_id F x)
                    (id_disp
                       (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                          (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))) ;; 
                  id_disp
                    (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                       (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))))) ;; 
         id_disp
           (pr1 G₃ (F x)
              (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))%mor_disp)) =

  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[

            (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))

  (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
     (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
  (maponpaths # F
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x))
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
           (pr1 G₃ (F x)
              (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
        (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x))
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
            G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
            (# F)%cat z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
                           (pr1 G₂ (F x)
                              (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
           (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof
              x)
           (transportf
              (mor_disp
                 (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
                 (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
              (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
              (transportf
                 (mor_disp
                    (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
                    (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                       (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
                 (maponpaths
                    (compose ((# F)%cat (id₁ x)))
                    (! functor_id F x))
                 (transportf
                    (mor_disp
                       (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                          (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
                       (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                          (pr1 G₂ (F x)
                             (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
                    (cancel_postcomposition
                       (id₁ (F x)) ((# F)%cat (id₁ x))
                       (id₁ (F x)) (! functor_id F x))
                    (id_disp
                       (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                          (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))) ;; 
                     id_disp
                       (pr1 G₃ (F x)
                          (pr1 G₂ (F x)
                             (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))))) ;; 
         id_disp
           (pr1 G₃ (F x)
              (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))%mor_disp)) =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
   # F z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
            (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
           (pr1 G₃ (F x)
              (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
        (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x))
        (transportf
           (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
            G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
            (# F)%cat z] G₃ (F x)
                           (pr1 G₂ (F x)
                              (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
           (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof
              x)
           (transportf
              (mor_disp
                 (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
                 (G₃ (F x)
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
              (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
              (transportf
                 (mor_disp
                    (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
                    (G₃ (F x)
                       (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
                 (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x))
                    ((# F)%cat (id₁ x))
                    ((# F)%cat (id₁ x))
                    (! functor_id F x))
                 (id_disp
                    (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))) ;; 
                  ♯ G₃
                    (transportf
                       (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
                        pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx) -->[
                        z] pr1 G₂ (F x)
                             (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))
                       (! functor_id F x)
                       (id_disp
                          (pr1 G₂ (F x)
                             (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))))) ;; 
         id_disp
           (pr1 G₃ (F x)
              (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))%mor_disp))

G₂: opfib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
G₃: opfib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₃, D₄ ⟧
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf
  (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
     (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
  (! id_right (# F (id₁ x)) @
   maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
     (! functor_id F x) @
   ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x) @
   maponpaths # F
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x))
  (transportf
     (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
      G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
      # F z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
               (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
     (transportf
        (mor_disp
           (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
           (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))))
        (! id_right (id₁ (F x)) @
         cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x))
           (# F (id₁ x)) (id₁ (F x))
           (! functor_id F x) @
         maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x) @
         ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
        (id_disp
           (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))))) =
?b
C₁, C₂: bicat_of_univ_cats
F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧
D₁, D₂, D₃, D₄: opfib_slice_bicat C₂
G₁: opfib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₁, D₂ ⟧
G₂: opfib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₂, D₃ ⟧
G₃: opfib_slice_bicat C₂ ⟦ D₃, D₄ ⟧
x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
?b =
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
   # F z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
            (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportf
     (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
     (! id_right (# F (id₁ x)) @
      maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
        (! functor_id F x) @
      ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
         G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
         # F z] G₃ (F x)
                  (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
        (transportf
           (mor_disp
              (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
              (G₃ (F x)
                 (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x))
              (# F (id₁ x)) (# F (id₁ x))
              (! functor_id F x) @
            ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
           (id_disp
              (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))) ;; 
            ♯ G₃
              (transportf
                 (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
                  pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx) -->[
                  z] pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))
                 (! functor_id F x)
                 (id_disp
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))))%mor_disp)))

      cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x)) (# F (id₁ x))
        (id₁ (F x)) (! functor_id F x) @
      maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
        (! functor_id F x) @
      ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (id_disp
        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))))

xx: pr1 (reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
transportf
  (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
   G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
   # F z] pr1 G₃ (F x)
            (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)

     (mor_disp (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
     (! id_right (# F (id₁ x)) @
      maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
        (! functor_id F x) @
      ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (λ z : C₁ ⟦ x, x ⟧,
         G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)) -->[
         # F z] G₃ (F x)
                  (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))
        (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
        (transportf
           (mor_disp
              (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
              (G₃ (F x)
                 (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx))))
           (cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x))
              (# F (id₁ x)) (# F (id₁ x))
              (! functor_id F x) @
            ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))

              (G₃ (F x) (G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))) ;; 
            ♯ G₃

                 (id_disp
                    (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))))%mor_disp))) =

        apply transportf_reindex.

     (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
     (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))))
  ((! id_right (id₁ (F x)) @
    cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x)) (# F (id₁ x))
      (id₁ (F x)) (! functor_id F x) @

      (! functor_id F x) @

     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x) @

     (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (pr1 G₁ (F x) xx)))) =
transportf
  (mor_disp
     (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx)))
     (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))))
  ((! id_right (id₁ (F x)) @
    cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x)) (# F (id₁ x))
      (id₁ (F x)) (! functor_id F x) @
    maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
      (! functor_id F x) @
    ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x)) @
   maponpaths # F
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x) @
   ! id_right (# F (id₁ x)) @
   maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
     (! functor_id F x) @
   ! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x) @
   maponpaths # F
     (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x))
  (id_disp (pr1 G₃ (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))))

  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)
  (transportb
     (mor_disp (H (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))
        (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))
     (functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (♯ H
        (transportb
           (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
            pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)
           (functor_id F x) (α (F x) xx)) ;; transportb
                                               (λ 
                                                z : 
                                                 C₂
                                                 ⟦ 
                                                 F x,
                                                 F x ⟧,
                                                pr1 H
                                                 (F x)
                                                 (pr1
                                                 G₂
                                                 (F x)
                                                 xx) -->[
                                                z] 
                                                pr1 H
                                                 (F x)
                                                 (pr1
                                                 G₂
                                                 (F x)
                                                 xx))
                                               (functor_id
                                                 F x)
                                               (id_disp
                                                 (pr1
                                                 H
                                                 (F x)
                                                 (pr1
                                                 G₂
                                                 (F x)
                                                 xx))))%mor_disp)

        (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))
     (! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x))
     (transportf
        (mor_disp (H (F x) (G₁ (F x) xx))
           (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))
        (maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x)))
           (! functor_id F x))
        (♯ H
           (transportf
              (λ z : C₂ ⟦ F x, F x ⟧,
               pr1 G₁ (F x) xx -->[ z] pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)
              (! functor_id F x) (α (F x) xx)) ;; 
         id_disp (pr1 H (F x) (pr1 G₂ (F x) xx)))%mor_disp)) =
?b

        apply transportf_reindex.

F: bicat_of_univ_cats ⟦ C₁, C₂ ⟧

maponpaths # (functor_identity C₂) (! functor_id F x) @
! id_right (# F (id₁ x)) @
maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x))) (! functor_id F x) @
! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x) @
maponpaths # F
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x) =
! id_left (id₁ (F x)) @
cancel_postcomposition (id₁ (F x)) (# F (id₁ x))
  (id₁ (F x)) (! functor_id F x) @
maponpaths (compose (# F (id₁ x))) (! functor_id F x) @
! functor_comp F (id₁ x) (id₁ x) @
maponpaths # F
  (disp_nat_trans_over_id_comp_data_subproof x)

      apply homset_property.
  Qed.

     reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data G₁ G₂)

  (PseudoFunctorBicat.psfunctor_comp
     reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data G₁ G₂)

x: C₁
xx: pr1 (reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data D₁) x
is_z_iso_disp
  (nat_z_iso_pointwise_z_iso
     (nat_z_iso_id (functor_identity C₁)) x)

     reindex_opfib_psfunctor_data G₁ G₂ x xx)

      apply (@id_is_z_iso_disp _ (reindex_disp_cat F (pr1 D₃))).
  Defined.
